However, if you do not wish to participate in this survey, you may inform the research company personnel when you receive the call, but we sincerely hope that you will participate as your view and feedback is valuable to us.\n<br>\n<br>\nWe wish to thank you in advance for your time as well as your valuable feedback and cooperation in making this survey a success. Should you have any enquiries about this survey, please email us at <a href=\"mailto:customer.service@rhbgroup.com\">customer.service@rhbgroup.com</a></div><div class=\"modal-footer text-right\"><button class=\"btn btn-ghost btn-blue\" data-dismiss=\"modal\">CLOSE</button></div></div></div></div><div id=\"Bank-Negara-Malaysia-BNM-Supplementary-Notice-on-Foreign-Exchange-Administration-Rules-Supplementary-Notice-on-FEA-Rules\" class=\"modal modal-overlay fade\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"dialog\"><div class=\"modal-dialog modal-lg\"><div class=\"modal-content\"><button class=\"close\" data-dismiss=\"modal\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><span class=\"rhb-glyph-icon-times\"></span></button><div class=\"modal-header\"><h2 class=\"modal-title\">Bank Negara Malaysia (“BNM”) Supplementary Notice on Foreign Exchange Administration Rules (“Supplementary Notice on FEA Rules”)</h2></div><div class=\"modal-body\"><p>Dear Valued  Customer </p>\n<p><strong>Re: Bank Negara Malaysia (“BNM”) Supplementary  Notice on Foreign Exchange Administration Rules (“Supplementary Notice on FEA  Rules”)</strong><strong> </strong></p>\n<p>As you are  aware, the Supplementary Notice on FEA Rules issued by BNM has introduced new  measures (effective 5 December 2016) to promote the development of the  Malaysian Financial Market. To facilitate the new measures introduced we would  like to highlight to you the following:- </p>\n<ol>\n    <li>The existing Foreign Currency Account I (“FCA I”) and Foreign Currency Account II (“FCA II”), have been replaced with the Trade Foreign Currency Account (“Trade FCA”) and Investment Foreign Currency Account (“Investment FCA”), respectively.  Accordingly, starting 5 December 2016, RHB will be re-classifying the Multi Currency Accounts (“MCA”) as follows:-<br>\n    <br>\n    <ul>\n        <li>For Individuals, the MCA-Individual Account (INDA) and MCA-Educational and Employment Account (EDEA) will be re-classified as Investment MCA (Investment FCA under BNM new measures).</li>\n        <li>For Entities, the MCA-Export Proceeds (EXPA) will be re-classified as Trade MCA (Trade FCA under BNM measures), while, MCA-Non-Export Proceeds (NEPA) will be re-classified as Investment MCA (Investment FCA under BNM new measures). </li>\n        <br>\n    </ul>\n    </li>\n    <li>Under the Supplementary Notice on FEA Rules, a resident exporter is allowed to retain up to 25% of export proceeds in foreign currency while a minimum of 75% of the export proceeds must be converted into Ringgit. For this purpose, RHB shall proceed to convert 75% of the foreign currency export proceeds received in your Trade MCA into Ringgit using the published rates or contracted rates, if RHB does not receive any conversion request from the resident exporter client:<br>\n    <br>\n    <ol style=\"list-style-type: lower-roman;\">\n        <li>by 4.00 p.m. the same business day for foreign currency proceeds received before 12.00 p.m.;</li>\n        <li>by 4.00 p.m. the next business day for foreign currency proceeds received from 12.00 p.m. onwards; or</li>\n        <li>the next business day for foreign currency proceeds received on a public holiday.</li>\n    </ol>\n    </li>\n    <p>As any incoming funds deposited into the Trade MCA will be deemed as export proceeds, it is advisable for affected customers to open an Investment MCA for all other purposes of foreign currency, excluding trade.</p>\n    <li>The remaining 25% of the Foreign Currency export proceeds can be retained in the Trade MCA for purposes of loan repayments / financing payments or import payments or for transfer to Investment MCA, subject to conditions. Customers may request to simultaneously reconvert foreign currency proceeds at the same rate on the same day for purposes of loan repayments / financing payments, import payments and permitted payment in foreign currency between residents of Malaysia up to 31 March 2017.</li>\n    <br>\n    <li>Customers who wish to retain more than 25% of their foreign currency export proceeds in the Trade MCA for import obligations or loan repayments / financing payments or exceed the limit for transfer to Investment MCA, must obtain BNM’s prior written approval.</li>\n    <br>\n    <li>Please note that customers who wish to place the Ringgit from the conversion of the 75% foreign currency export proceeds into the Money Market Term Deposit – Special Deposit Facility (MMTD - SDF) account / Commodity Murabahah Money Market Deposit-i – Special Deposit Facility (CMMMD-i – SDF) account will enjoy a deposit rate of 3.25% p.a., based on the end of day balances in the MMTD-SDF / CMMMD-i – SDF. Please refer to your Relationship Manager for further details in relation to the said MMTD-SDF / CMMMD-i – SDF account. </li>\n    <br>\n    <li>Resident entities and individuals with Ringgit borrowings can invest in foreign currency assets onshore and offshore from Ringgit conversion subject to a limit of RM 50 million and RM 1 million in aggregate per calendar year respectively. Resident entities and individuals without Ringgit borrowings will continue to enjoy the flexibility of investing in foreign currency investment from Ringgit conversion both onshore and offshore up to any amount. </li>\n</ol>\n<p>The above measures only apply to residents of Malaysia. In this regard, in the event of any change in your residential status, please notify us immediately.</p>\n<p>For more  information on the above measures, kindly refer to this link at BNM’s website:<br>\n<a href=\"http://www.bnm.gov.my/index.php?ch=en_announcement&amp;pg=en_announcement&amp;ac=481\" target=\"_blank\">Supplementary  Notice on Foreign Exchange Administration Rules – Measures to Promote the  Development of Malaysian Financial Market</a></p>\n<p>Should you require further clarification, please do  not hesitate to contact our respective branches or Relationship Managers and we  will be more than happy to assist you. </p></div><div class=\"modal-footer text-right\"><button class=\"btn btn-ghost btn-blue\" data-dismiss=\"modal\">CLOSE</button></div></div></div></div><div id=\"Bank-Negara-Malaysia-Notification-on-Fraudster\" class=\"modal modal-overlay fade\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"dialog\"><div class=\"modal-dialog modal-lg\"><div class=\"modal-content\"><button class=\"close\" data-dismiss=\"modal\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><span class=\"rhb-glyph-icon-times\"></span></button><div class=\"modal-header\"><h2 class=\"modal-title\"></h2></div><div class=\"modal-body\"><div class=\"modal-header\">\n<h2 class=\"modal-title\">ALERT!</h2>\n</div>\n<div class=\"modal-body\">\n<p><strong><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">BEWARE</span></strong> of any message that claims to be from Bank Negara Malaysia (BNM), stating pending payment to your account and requesting security verification. Please note that the URLs listed are fake and will direct you to an unsecure site.\n<br>\n<br>\n<strong><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\">\nPLEASE DO NOT</span></strong> click on any suspicious URLs and be vigilant upon retrieving such URLs.\n</p>\n</div></div><div class=\"modal-footer text-right\"><button class=\"btn btn-ghost btn-blue\" data-dismiss=\"modal\">CLOSE</button></div></div></div></div><div id=\"Important-Notice-Integration-of-RHB-Easy-with-RHB-Bank-Branch-RHB-Sales-Centre-wef-1-Nov-2016-onward\" class=\"modal modal-overlay fade\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"dialog\"><div class=\"modal-dialog modal-lg\"><div class=\"modal-content\"><button class=\"close\" data-dismiss=\"modal\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><span class=\"rhb-glyph-icon-times\"></span></button><div class=\"modal-header\"><h2 class=\"modal-title\"></h2></div><div class=\"modal-body\"><div class=\"modal-header\">\n<h2 class=\"modal-title\">ANNOUNCEMENT</h2>\n</div>\n<div class=\"modal-body\">\n<p>Dear Valued Customer,</p>\n<p>In line with the RHB Banking Group’s effort to increase operational efficiency, we are integrating our Easy outlets with the nearest RHB Bank branch/ RHB Sales Centre effective 1 November 2016 onward. <br>\n<br>\nAll our customer’s accounts and facilities will remain unchanged.
